0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe \u003ccode\u003eMemoryStorage\u003c/code\u003e function creates (or returns) a storage object implementing the W3C Web Storage API.\nBy default, scripts share a \u003ccode\u003eglobal\u003c/code\u003e storage object, so scripts can access and mutate each other's store\nobject. To have MemoryStorage create a storage object that is isolated from other scripts, you pass in\na unique ID which acts as a namespace:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"var isolated = new MemoryStorage('my-app'); // isolated from other scripts, recommended.\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003evar\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eisolated\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003enew\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003eMemoryStorage\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e(\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e'my-app'\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e)\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e;\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e// isolated from other scripts, recommended.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf you don't pass in an ID, or use the ID \u003ccode\u003e'global'\u003c/code\u003e, you get a globally shared storage object:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"var global = new MemoryStorage(); // will default to a globally shared storage object.\nvar global2 = new MemoryStorage('global'); // effectively same as above\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003eMemoryStorage\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e(\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e)\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eglobal2\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003enew\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe Web Storage API is pretty small. For discovering which key-value pairs are available within\nthe storage object, you basically only have the \u003ccode\u003elength\u003c/code\u003e property and the \u003ccode\u003ekey(idx)\u003c/code\u003e function.\nThe same applies to reading, writing and removing keys. You have the functions \u003ccode\u003egetItem\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003esetItem\u003c/code\u003e\nand \u003ccode\u003eremoveItem\u003c/code\u003e and there is \u003ccode\u003eclear\u003c/code\u003e but that pretty much sums it up.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn practice there are many other ways to interact with storage objects, such as \u003ccode\u003estore[myKey] = myValue\u003c/code\u003e,\nor \u003ccode\u003edelete store[myKey]\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003eObject.keys(store)\u003c/code\u003e etc, but please remember that when you use these\nconstructs, you venture outside the interface provided by the Web Storage API and run the risk of\nincompatibility.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis project is committed to be as compatible as possible with the \u003ccode\u003elocalStorage\u003c/code\u003e object present in\nreal-life browsers, but due to inherent limitations to the Javascript language, it's impossible to\nguarantee the same behavior in all instances if you go beyond the Web Storage API.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" memorystorage \u003csub\u003e\u003csup\u003ev0.12.0\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/sub\u003e","Memory-backed storage that implements the [Web Storage API](http://www.w3.org/TR/webstorage/), making it a drop-in replacement for `localStorage` and `sessionStorage` in environments where these are not available.","[Project website](http://download.github.io/memorystorage)","","[![npm](https://img.shields.io/npm/v/memorystorage.svg?maxAge=2592000)](https://npmjs.com/package/memorystorage)","[![license](https://img.shields.io/npm/l/memorystorage.svg)](https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/4.0/)","[![travis](https://img.shields.io/travis/Download/memorystorage.svg)](https://travis-ci.org/Download/memorystorage)","[![greenkeeper](https://img.shields.io/david/Download/memorystorage.svg?maxAge=2592000)](https://greenkeeper.io/)","![mind BLOWN](https://img.shields.io/badge/mind-BLOWN-ff69b4.svg)","","\u003csup\u003e\u003csub\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003csub\u003e.\u003c/sub\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/sub\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e","","![logo](https://rawgit.com/download/memorystorage/0.12.0/memorystorage.png)","","\u003csup\u003e\u003csub\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003csub\u003e.\u003c/sub\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/sub\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e","","","## Installation","**For Node**","```sh","npm install --save memorystorage","```","","**For browsers**","## Include on your page","`memorystorage` can be used directly from CDN, from a local script file, or from a module loader.","","### CDN","This is by far the easiest method and gives good performance to boost. Use this if you are in doubt.","```xml","\u003cscript src=\"https://cdn.rawgit.com/download/memorystorage/0.12.0/dist/memorystorage.min.js\"\u003e\u003c/script\u003e","```","","### Local script file","Download memorystorage.min.js, place it in a folder `lib` in the root of your website and include it like this:","```xml","\u003cscript src=\"lib/memorystorage.min.js\"\u003e\u003c/script\u003e","```","","#### Download","* [memorystorage.umd.js](https://cdn.rawgit.com/download/memorystorage/0.12.0/dist/memorystorage.umd.js) (~4kB, commented)","* [memorystorage.min.js](https://cdn.rawgit.com/download/memorystorage/0.12.0/dist/memorystorage.min.js) (~2kB, minified)","* [memorystorage.min.js.map](https://cdn.rawgit.com/download/memorystorage/0.12.0/dist/memorystorage.min.js.map) (~2kB, debug map file)","","### Module loaders","Memorystorage implements the Universal Module Pattern and as such, is available to be consumed","from Node modules as well as via an AMD loader such as RequireJS.","","#### Node","```javascript","var MemoryStorage = require('memorystorage');","// here, the MemoryStorage function is available","var myStorage = new MemoryStorage('my-app');","```","","#### AMD","```javascript","define(['memorystorage'], function(MemoryStorage){","\t// here, the MemoryStorage function is available","\tvar myStorage = new MemoryStorage('my-app');","});","```","To be able to load MemoryStorage from CDN as an AMD module, configure the CDN url like so \u003csmall\u003e(note the absence of `.js` in the url)\u003c/small\u003e:","```javascript","require.config({","\tpaths: {","\t\t'memorystorage': 'https://cdn.rawgit.com/download/memorystorage/0.12.0/dist/memorystorage.min'","\t}","});","```","","#### ES2015","```js","import MemoryStorage from 'memorystorage'","// here, the MemoryStorage function is available","const myStorage = new MemoryStorage('my-app');","```","","## Create a memory storage object","The `MemoryStorage` function creates (or returns) a storage object implementing the W3C Web Storage API.","By default, scripts share a `global` storage object, so scripts can access and mutate each other's store","object. To have MemoryStorage create a storage object that is isolated from other scripts, you pass in","a unique ID which acts as a namespace:","","```javascript","var isolated = new MemoryStorage('my-app'); // isolated from other scripts, recommended.","```","","If you don't pass in an ID, or use the ID `'global'`, you get a globally shared storage object:","","```javascript","var global = new MemoryStorage(); // will default to a globally shared storage object.","var global2 = new MemoryStorage('global'); // effectively same as above","```","","For your convenience, the constructor permits `new`-less invocation:","```javascript","var store = MemoryStorage('my-store');","var global = MemoryStorage();","```","","Instances of `MemoryStorage` expose an immutable `id` property that is set to","the id the store was created with:","","```javascript","alert(store.id); // alerts 'my-store'","alert(global.id); // alerts 'global'","```","","## Use it","```javascript","store.setItem('myString', 'Hello MemoryStorage!');","store.myObject = JSON.stringify({my: 'object'}));","alert(store.getItem('My string')); // alerts 'Hello MemoryStorage!'","alert(store['My string']); // alerts 'Hello MemoryStorage!'","alert(store.length); // alerts '2'","alert(store.key(1)); // alerts 'My object'","store.removeItem('My string');","alert(store.length); // alerts '1'","store.clear();","alert(store.length); // alerts '0'","```","","## Staying within the Web Storage API","The Web Storage API is pretty small. For discovering which key-value pairs are available within","the storage object, you basically only have the `length` property and the `key(idx)` function.","The same applies to reading, writing and removing keys. You have the functions `getItem`, `setItem`","and `removeItem` and there is `clear` but that pretty much sums it up.","","In practice there are many other ways to interact with storage objects, such as `store[myKey] = myValue`,","or `delete store[myKey]` or `Object.keys(store)` etc, but please remember that when you use these","constructs, you venture outside the interface provided by the Web Storage API and run the risk of","incompatibility.","","This project is committed to be as compatible as possible with the `localStorage` object present in","real-life browsers, but due to inherent limitations to the Javascript language, it's impossible to","guarantee the same behavior in all instances if you go beyond the Web Storage API.","","### Example of going outside of the API","Here is some code to print all the keys and values in the `store` object that does not limit itself","to the Web Storage API:","```js","var keys = Object.keys(store);","for (var i=0; i\u003ckeys.length; i++) {","\tvar key = keys(i);","\tvar value = store[key];","\tconsole.info(key + ': ' + value);","}","```","","### Example of staying within the API","Here is the same code, rewritten to stay within the API:","```js","for (var i=0; i\u003cstore.length; i++) {","\tvar key = store.key(i);","\tvar value = store.getItem(key);","\tconsole.info(key + ': ' + value);","}","```","","## Beyond the Web Storage API","MemoryStorage is type-agnostic; it doesn't care about the type of data you store.","If you want to remain within the Web Storage API, you should only read and write strings,","however if you want you can store other types just as well:","```javascript","store.myObject = {my: 'object'};","alert(store.myObject.my); // alerts 'object'","var tree = {","\tnested: {","\t\tobjects: {","\t\t\tworking: 'Sure!'","\t\t}","\t}","}","store.setItem('tree', tree);","alert(store.tree.nested.objects.working); // alerts 'Sure!'","```","","## Contributors","I'd like to draw your attention to the people that contributed to this project with bug reports,","documentation, pull requests or other forms of support.","* [Stafford Brunk](https://github.com/wingrunr21)","\t * [Push v0.9.10 to NPM #1](https://github.com/Download/memorystorage/issues/1) (reported issue)","* [Matthias Seemann](https://github.com/semmel):","   * [Items with store API key names are considered by key() #3](https://github.com/Download/memorystorage/pull/3) (code contribution)","   * [getItem should return null for not-existing keys #4](https://github.com/Download/memorystorage/pull/4) (code contribution)","* [Chris Smola](https://github.com/Smolations)","   * [Add npm install to README #5](https://github.com/Download/memorystorage/issues/5) (reported issue)","* [Corentin Minne](https://github.com/CorentinMinne)","   * [Invalid exports in package.json #14](https://github.com/Download/memorystorage/issues/14) (code contribution)","","## Copyright","©2016 by Stijn de Witt and contributors. BlobContent-module__blobContentSectionMarkdown__mPLOK" style="margin-top:46px"><div class="js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned BlobContent-module__markdownBlob__T8jpG" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">memorystorage <sub><sup>v0.12.0</sup></sub></h1><a id="user-content-memorystorage-v0120" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: memorystorage " href="#memorystorage-v0120"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Memory-backed storage that implements the <a href="http://www.w3.org/TR/webstorage/" rel="nofollow">Web Storage API</a>, making it a drop-in replacement for <code>localStorage</code> and <code>sessionStorage</code> in environments where these are not available.
<a href="http://download.github.io/memorystorage" rel="nofollow">Project website</a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://npmjs.com/package/memorystorage" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/e35f17d9ed008914167afc6ca07100c7306efe69a179f34904f288d89cf0fa62/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6e706d2f762f6d656d6f727973746f726167652e7376673f6d61784167653d32353932303030" alt="npm" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/npm/v/memorystorage.svg?maxAge=2592000" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/4.0/" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/5e42e02fd91f71524bbdbc07c8b1e5e9d9a10b9a30049b25c5684565606defca/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6e706d2f6c2f6d656d6f727973746f726167652e737667" alt="license" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/npm/l/memorystorage.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>

<p dir="auto"><sup><sub><sup><sub>.</sub></sup></sub></sup></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>For Node</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npm install --save memorystorage"><pre>npm install --save memorystorage</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>For browsers</strong></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Include on your page</h2><a id="user-content-include-on-your-page" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Include on your page" href="#include-on-your-page"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>memorystorage</code> can be used directly from CDN, from a local script file, or from a module loader.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">CDN</h3><a id="user-content-cdn" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: CDN" href="#cdn"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This is by far the easiest method and gives good performance to boost. Use this if you are in doubt.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-xml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;script src=&quot;https://cdn.rawgit.com/download/memorystorage/0.12.0/dist/memorystorage.min.js&quot;&gt;&lt;/script&gt;"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-ent">script</span> <span class="pl-e">src</span>=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://cdn.rawgit.com/download/memorystorage/0.12.0/dist/memorystorage.min.js<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>&gt;&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">script</span>&gt;</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Local script file</h3><a id="user-content-local-script-file" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Local script file" href="#local-script-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Download memorystorage.min.js, place it in a folder <code>lib</code> in the root of your website and include it like this:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-xml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;script src=&quot;lib/memorystorage.min.js&quot;&gt;&lt;/script&gt;"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-ent">script</span> <span class="pl-e">src</span>=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>lib/memorystorage.min.js<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>&gt;&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">script</span>&gt;</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Download</h4><a id="user-content-download" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Download" href="#download"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Module loaders</h3><a id="user-content-module-loaders" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Module loaders" href="#module-loaders"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Memorystorage implements the Universal Module Pattern and as such, is available to be consumed
from Node modules as well as via an AMD loader such as RequireJS.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Node</h4><a id="user-content-node" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Node" href="#node"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="var MemoryStorage = require('memorystorage');
// here, the MemoryStorage function is available
var myStorage = new MemoryStorage('my-app');"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">MemoryStorage</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">require</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'memorystorage'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-c">// here, the MemoryStorage function is available</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">myStorage</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">MemoryStorage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-app'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">AMD</h4><a id="user-content-amd" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: AMD" href="#amd"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="define(['memorystorage'], function(MemoryStorage){
	// here, the MemoryStorage function is available
	var myStorage = new MemoryStorage('my-app');
});"><pre><span class="pl-en">define</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'memorystorage'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-v">MemoryStorage</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
	<span class="pl-c">// here, the MemoryStorage function is available</span>
	<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">myStorage</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">MemoryStorage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-app'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">To be able to load MemoryStorage from CDN as an AMD module, configure the CDN url like so (note the absence of <code>.js</code> in the url):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="require.config({
	paths: {
		'memorystorage': 'https://cdn.rawgit.com/download/memorystorage/0.12.0/dist/memorystorage.min'
	}
});"><pre><span class="pl-en">require</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">config</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
	<span class="pl-c1">paths</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
		<span class="pl-s">'memorystorage'</span>: <span class="pl-s">'https://cdn.rawgit.com/download/memorystorage/0.12.0/dist/memorystorage.min'</span>
	<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">ES2015</h4><a id="user-content-es2015" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ES2015" href="#es2015"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import MemoryStorage from 'memorystorage'
// here, the MemoryStorage function is available
const myStorage = new MemoryStorage('my-app');"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">MemoryStorage</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'memorystorage'</span>
<span class="pl-c">// here, the MemoryStorage function is available</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">myStorage</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">MemoryStorage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-app'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Create a memory storage object</h2><a id="user-content-create-a-memory-storage-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Create a memory storage object" href="#create-a-memory-storage-object"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>MemoryStorage</code> function creates (or returns) a storage object implementing the W3C Web Storage API.
By default, scripts share a <code>global</code> storage object, so scripts can access and mutate each other's store
object. To have MemoryStorage create a storage object that is isolated from other scripts, you pass in
a unique ID which acts as a namespace:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="var isolated = new MemoryStorage('my-app'); // isolated from other scripts, recommended."><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">isolated</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">MemoryStorage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-app'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// isolated from other scripts, recommended.</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If you don't pass in an ID, or use the ID <code>'global'</code>, you get a globally shared storage object:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="var global = new MemoryStorage(); // will default to a globally shared storage object.
var global2 = new MemoryStorage('global'); // effectively same as above"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">global</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">MemoryStorage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// will default to a globally shared storage object.</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">global2</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">MemoryStorage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'global'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// effectively same as above</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">For your convenience, the constructor permits <code>new</code>-less invocation:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="var store = MemoryStorage('my-store');
var global = MemoryStorage();"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">store</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">MemoryStorage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-store'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">global</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">MemoryStorage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Instances of <code>MemoryStorage</code> expose an immutable <code>id</code> property that is set to
the id the store was created with:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="alert(store.id); // alerts 'my-store'
alert(global.id); // alerts 'global'"><pre><span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// alerts 'my-store'</span>
<span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">global</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// alerts 'global'</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Use it</h2><a id="user-content-use-it" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Use it" href="#use-it"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="store.setItem('myString', 'Hello MemoryStorage!');
store.myObject = JSON.stringify({my: 'object'}));
alert(store.getItem('My string')); // alerts 'Hello MemoryStorage!'
alert(store['My string']); // alerts 'Hello MemoryStorage!'
alert(store.length); // alerts '2'
alert(store.key(1)); // alerts 'My object'
store.removeItem('My string');
alert(store.length); // alerts '1'
store.clear();
alert(store.length); // alerts '0'"><pre><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">setItem</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'myString'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'Hello MemoryStorage!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">myObject</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">JSON</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">stringify</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">my</span>: <span class="pl-s">'object'</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">getItem</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'My string'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// alerts 'Hello MemoryStorage!'</span>
<span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'My string'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// alerts 'Hello MemoryStorage!'</span>
<span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// alerts '2'</span>
<span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">key</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// alerts 'My object'</span>
<span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">removeItem</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'My string'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// alerts '1'</span>
<span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">clear</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// alerts '0'</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Staying within the Web Storage API</h2><a id="user-content-staying-within-the-web-storage-api" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Staying within the Web Storage API" href="#staying-within-the-web-storage-api"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Web Storage API is pretty small. For discovering which key-value pairs are available within
the storage object, you basically only have the <code>length</code> property and the <code>key(idx)</code> function.
The same applies to reading, writing and removing keys. You have the functions <code>getItem</code>, <code>setItem</code>
and <code>removeItem</code> and there is <code>clear</code> but that pretty much sums it up.</p>
<p dir="auto">In practice there are many other ways to interact with storage objects, such as <code>store[myKey] = myValue</code>,
or <code>delete store[myKey]</code> or <code>Object.keys(store)</code> etc, but please remember that when you use these
constructs, you venture outside the interface provided by the Web Storage API and run the risk of
incompatibility.</p>
<p dir="auto">This project is committed to be as compatible as possible with the <code>localStorage</code> object present in
real-life browsers, but due to inherent limitations to the Javascript language, it's impossible to
guarantee the same behavior in all instances if you go beyond the Web Storage API.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Example of going outside of the API</h3><a id="user-content-example-of-going-outside-of-the-api" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example of going outside of the API" href="#example-of-going-outside-of-the-api"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Here is some code to print all the keys and values in the <code>store</code> object that does not limit itself
to the Web Storage API:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="var keys = Object.keys(store);
for (var i=0; i&lt;keys.length; i++) {
	var key = keys(i);
	var value = store[key];
	console.info(key + ': ' + value);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">keys</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">keys</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s1">keys</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-c1">++</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
	<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">key</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">keys</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
	<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">key</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
	<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">info</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">key</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s">': '</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Example of staying within the API</h3><a id="user-content-example-of-staying-within-the-api" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example of staying within the API" href="#example-of-staying-within-the-api"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Here is the same code, rewritten to stay within the API:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="for (var i=0; i&lt;store.length; i++) {
	var key = store.key(i);
	var value = store.getItem(key);
	console.info(key + ': ' + value);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-c1">++</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
	<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">key</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">key</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
	<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">getItem</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">key</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
	<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">info</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">key</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s">': '</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Beyond the Web Storage API</h2><a id="user-content-beyond-the-web-storage-api" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Beyond the Web Storage API" href="#beyond-the-web-storage-api"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">MemoryStorage is type-agnostic; it doesn't care about the type of data you store.
If you want to remain within the Web Storage API, you should only read and write strings,
however if you want you can store other types just as well:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="store.myObject = {my: 'object'};
alert(store.myObject.my); // alerts 'object'
var tree = {
	nested: {
		objects: {
			working: 'Sure!'
		}
	}
}
store.setItem('tree', tree);
alert(store.tree.nested.objects.working); // alerts 'Sure!'"><pre><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">myObject</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">my</span>: <span class="pl-s">'object'</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">myObject</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">my</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// alerts 'object'</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">tree</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
	<span class="pl-c1">nested</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
		<span class="pl-c1">objects</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
			<span class="pl-c1">working</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Sure!'</span>
		<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
	<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">setItem</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'tree'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">tree</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">store</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">tree</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">nested</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">objects</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">working</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// alerts 'Sure!'</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Contributors</h2><a id="user-content-contributors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Contributors" href="#contributors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
